 yah syndicate feed se sidhe prakashit kii gai he) Manjur Ehtesham is the most important storyteller of our time
 unka janm 3 april, 1948 ko bhopal main hua tha
 Householders wanted him to become an engineer, but he had to become a writer
 so ejineering kii padhai adhuri chhot gai
 First he started selling medicines and then started selling furniture
 baad main interior debor kaa bhi kaam karne lage
 But the writing continued in every round
 pehali kahani 'ramadan main maut' saal 1973 main chhapi, to pehla upanyaas 'kuch din or' saal 1976 main prakashit hua
 Due to writing, he has been decorated with Vagishwari Award, Pahl Samman and Padma Shri
 unki khaasiyat yah he ki unki rachanaaen kisi chamatkaar ke liye vyagr nahin dikhti, balki ve anek antervirodhon or traasadiyon ke baavjood 'chamatkaar kii tarah bache jivan' kaa aakhyaan rachati hai
 Manjur Ehtesham is a narrator who expresses the dialectical reality of middle class Indian society in a remarkable craft
 parichit yatharth ke adekhe konon-antaron ko apni rachanashiltaa se adubhut kahani main badal dete hai
 Middle class Muslim society has been appearing in the stories of Manjur Ehtesham with all their concern, consciousness and authenticity
 sthaniyata unke kathanak kaa swabhaav he or vyapak manushyata unka nishkarsh he
 This is the reason why he has come from popular novels like 'dastan-e-lapata', 'kuch Din Aur', 'drought Banyan', 'basharat Manzil', 'pahar Dhalte' and the anthology 'tasbeeh', 'tamasha and other stories' We take a better picture of our society
 aaj manzur ehteshaam ke janmdin par sahitya ajtak unki aupnyasik kriti 'madrasa' kaa ansh aapako padhaa rahaa
 'madrasa' is a pleasant intervention in the rhythmic landscape of contemporary Hindi novels
 yah upanyaas yah sthapit karata he ki sirf kahani bataa dena or prachlit vimarshon kii jumalebaji kaa baghaar daalate hue 'polyticali karact' morche par seenaa taan kar khadey ho janaa hi achche upanyaas kii guarantee nahin he
 Every novel has to invent its own rhythm in its language and structure, and this is what makes it part of the minds and minds of the reader for decades and centuries
 upanyaas 'madrasa' safaltaapurvak is jimmedaari ko anjaam detaa he
 Moving through different phases of the country and period, the novel goes through the process of internal and external changes of its characters, walking around the trails of memories; It is with those questions that time keeps on planting within us and also with the machines whose responsibility is never easy to decide
 kisi bhi umdaa rachana ko lekar yah kahana kabhi sambhav nahin hota ki iskaa uddeshy amuk he, athwa isse hamen amuk sandesh praapt hota he

 maafee kii yah yojana sabhi kisaanon ke liye nahin thi

 tippaniyan Official sources said that the jawans have been asked to increase vigil and surprise checks

 isamen yatriyon ke metal detector daravaaje se andar jane ke pehle bhi atirikt surakshakarmi jaanch karte hai

 upi chunaav prachaar ko lekar aisa bahut kam hi hoga jise likhaa naa ja chukaa ho yaa kaha naa ja chukaa ho
 As far as recollection goes, there would not have been such an assembly election in which such a large number of journalists have seen every electoral ups and downs with a political microscope like this
 pichley 15 din maine pashchimi uttar pradesh, bundelkhand or avadh ke alag-alag hisson kii yatraaen karte gujaarey
 During these visits i got an opportunity to spend time with Amit Shah, Rajnath Singh, Akhilesh Yadav, Mulayam Singh Yadav, Prashant Kishore and some more important veterans of UP elections
 maine pradhanmantri narendra modi or congress upaadhyaksh rahul gandhi ke bhaashan bhi sune
 Also, whoever came in contact with me, i wanted to know from him what he thinks about the important contenders in the election and what he intends to do in the election
 maine jo anubhav kiya usee ke aadhaar par main nishkarsh rakh rahaa hum ki abhi tak kya ho chukaa he or aakhri chaar charnon main kya badlaav ho saktaa he
 As always this time also i do not intend to keep my neck on the chopping block, so i will avoid guessing who is winning in my opinion
 neeche die nichod main main swayan ko vahiin tak simit rakhuunga jahaan tak kisi gaiyr-pakshpaati paryvekshak kii had hoti he
 1
 upi main bijepi kaa bhavishya hindu ekajutata par tikapradhanmantri ne ravivaar ko fatehpur main die bhaashan main 'kabristaan banaam shmashaan ghat' kii bahes ko beshak tool diya ho, lekin bijepi ke anya sabhi netaaon ke bhaashanon main shuru se hi sampradayik gunj mukharata se sunai detii rahi he
 The main thrust of the BJP has been that the Samajwadi Party government spent the last 5 years in the minority community appeasement and now is the time to fix things
 bihar main karaari shikast se bijepi ne jo ahm sabak siikhaa he wo he ki party vikaas ko hi ahm mudde ke taur par pesh karti rahi, vahiin lalu or nitish ke majboot jaateey ankaganit ne bhagava party kii sambhaavnaaon ko puri tarah dubo diya
 Mohan Bhagwat's statement on reservation was blamed on the remaining hopes that Amit Shah had unified in 2014 by uniting non-yadav Other Backward Classes (OBC) and Extremely Backward Classes (MBC)
 bundelkhand ke vibhinn hisson main amit shah ke saath puraa din bitaane ke dauraan dekha ki shah ko prachaar ke dauraan sabase zyada taaliyaan or samarthan tabhi mila jab unhone rajya main boojadkhaanon par pratibandh lagane kii baat kahi
 Shah alleges that during the Akhilesh government, the abattoirs had a chance to flourish on a large scale
 pehle ye pashchimi uttar pradesh tak hi simit tha, lekin ab ye upi ke anya hisson main bhi fail gaya he
 Shah alleges that slaves along with other animals are also slaughtered in these slaughterhouses
 boojadkhaanon par pratibandh lagane ke vaade ke saath hi bijepi teen talaak ke mudde ko bhi jor-shor se uthaa rahi he
 The party is also alleging that Akhilesh was biased towards his supporters in laptop distribution
 bijepi netritv party ke prachaar abhiyaan main sampradayik put ko lekar jaraa bhi sankoch baratate nahin dikhaa
 Hindus can be voted by keeping their religious identity at the top of the mind, this is the key for BJP to win UP
 pehle teen charnon ke matdaan se bijepi ko jo feedback mila he, uske aadhaar par party maanati he ki usne hindu takaton ko bade paimaane par ekajute karne ke liye paryaapt kaam kiya he or yahi alpsankhyak samarthit vipaksh ko maat dene main sakasham rahegaa
 2
 samarthan ko lekar alpsankhyakon ke aakraamak dikhaave par pratikriya hona taypashchimi uttar pradesh ke kuch hisson se mili reports ke mutabik muslim yuvaaon ne shaharon or kasbon main espi-congress gathbandhan ke samarthan main motorcykilon par reliyaan nikaalin
 This development caused uneasiness to the coalition managers who wanted the minority community not to be very vocal about supporting the Samajwadi Party and the Congress
 gathbandhan ke ranneetikaar chaahate hai ki muslim shant rahe or apane samarthan kaa khulaa izhaar nahin kare
 Instead, they go and vote for the coalition on the polling day
 shuruyaat main kuch andeh the kialpsankhyakkiske paksh main vot karenge
 But according to the trends of the first three phases of voting, the minorities mostly supported the alliance
 iske apwaad ke taur par un siton ke naam liye ja sakate hai jahaan bispi ne majboot alpsankhyak ummidavaar khadey kiye
 a top alliance strategist says that the minority support for the 'secular alliance' was not as strong as it was seen in Bihar, but the voting tendency of Muslims was mostly in favor of the alliance
 bijepi ne yah baat failaane main puri takat jhonki ki alpsankhyak badi sankhya main gathbandhan ke liye vot kar rahe hai or hinduon ko gathbandhan ko jeetne se rokane ke liye ekajute hona chahie
 Aggressive display of support from minorities affects the mindset of the majority community and may affect some voters
 dhruvikaran kaa str kahin se bhi vaisaa nahin he jaisaa ki mujffarnagar dangon ke baad dikhaa tha, lekin hindu ekajutata nishchit taur par is vidhansabha chunaav main bada kaarak he
 If the BJP manages to cross the finishing line first, then a majority of solidarity will be behind its victory
 3
 Bhaiyamaniya: a state where governance is considered to be crooked, it is considered natural to run a strong anti-incumbency wave when the term of a Chief Minister is completed
 aisa sabhi partiyon ke mukhyamantriyon ke saath ab do dashak se hota aa rahaa he
 The reality is that many political pundits are also skeptical this time what will happen in UP
 aisi sthiti ke liye mukhya rup se akhilesh yadav kii sakaaratmak chhavi ko vajah mana ja saktaa he, jinhen unke samarthak bhaiya ke naam se bulaate hai
 Even voters who do not intend to vote for Akhilesh are not in a position to say anything negative about Akhilesh
 puure upi main akhilesh kii reliyon main josh se bhare unke yuva samarthakon kaa jamghat dekha ja saktaa he
 Bhaiyamaniya has penetrated among the youth, especially Yadavs and Muslims
 samarthakon ke bich akhilesh kii chhavi political rockstar jaisi he
 Akhilesh is the first Yadav leader who has created a positive image for himself outside the traditional vote bank of his party
 akhilesh jeeten yaa haaren lekin itnaa tay he ki wo uttar pradesh kii siyasat main lambey samay tak ek dhuree bane rahenge
 Like PM Modi, Akhilesh also takes a master class in marketing
 puure prachaar abhiyaan ke dauraan akhilesh ne apana sandesh sakaaratmak banaae rakhaa
 He kept himself away from the negativity that his opponents have been using to attack him
 akhilesh lakhanu kaa cheharaa badal chuke hai
 With the addition of agra-lucknow Expressway, the condition of roads has been better than before but still the roads in UP are the worst in the country
 upi main rojgaar paidaa karnaa badi samasya he, vahiin teji se badhati aabaadi rojgaar kii talash main hataash ho rahi he
 4
 modi ke sitare kii sabase tej chamakpradhanmantri ke taur par narendra modi ke kaarykaal ko kareeb 3 saal puure hone ja rahe hai, lekin modi ke aakarshan main koi kami nahin ai he
 This correspondent also heard several Modi rallies during the 2014 campaign
 2014 abhiyaan ke unmaadi shikhar se tulana kii jaae to josh ke str main thodi kami ai he lekin ab bhi modi ke liye utsukata barkaraar he
 For a prime minister who is in his mid-term, this achievement is remarkable
 kaarykaal kaa madhya hi wo samay hota he jab akasar satta virdohi rujhaan bananaa shuru hota he lekin abhi tak is virus ne modi ko nahin kaata he
 The good days may not have come, but people still have great faith in the Prime Minister
 unka maananaa he ki bharat kii samasyaon kaa samaadhaan pradhanmantri ke paas he
 No one wins the battle of UP but defeating Modi in the 2019 general election will be nothing short of impossible for the opposition
 5
 BJP leaders are not in favor of giving more importance to demonetisation
 Of course in interviews, the BJP leaders should say that if the 2017 election is considered a mandate on demonetisation then they have no problem
 duusari ore jamini hakeekat ye he ki bijepi netritv apni taraf se puri koshish kar rahaa he ki logon ko notebandi kaa dard dobaaraa yaad naa karaayaa jaae
 In the entire day i spent with Amit Shah, he addressed four rallies and did not mention demonetisation even once
 grih mantrirajnath sinhanotbandi par bole lekin wo bhi sabha ke aakhir main, khanaapurti ke andaaj main
 The BJP wants to give voters a message to move forward rather than reassuring voters on the benefits of demonetisation
 bijepi chaahati he ki matadaata samajhen ki unhone jo pidaa jheli wo bade rashtriya hit main he or aane vaale samay main isse arthvyavastha ko laabh hoga
 6
 chunaav par notebandi ke mudde kaa asar nahimodi ke virodhiyon, khaas taur par rahul gandhi, ne bada vakt logon ko notebandi kii pidaa yaad karaane main lagaaya
 They wanted demonetisation to be the main issue in this election
 lekin aisa hua nahin
 The business community is undoubtedly unhappy with the BJP for imposing demonetisation on them, but they are unlikely to vote for Modi's opponents
 aisi report ain ki jor-shor se apni vyathaa bataane vaale banie chunaav main alag rah sakate hai or bijepi se naakhush hone kii vajah se vot nahin dene kaa faisla le sakate hai, lekin matdaan vaale din ye samudaay bijepi ke liye vot detaa najar aayaa
 According to bjp's calculations, businessmen dislike the condition of law and order under socialists more than demonetisation
 notebandi kii vajah se bijepi ke khilaaf vot karne waalon kii sankhya itani nahin ki usase chunaav kaa nateeja hi palat jaae
 7
 rahul ne ranneeti ko sudharamine punjab chunaav prachaar abhiyaan ko cover karte vakt bhi kaha tha, ab phir kah rahaa hum ki rahul gandhi ne logon ke bich bolne kii kala ko pehle se sudhara he
 Their messages are now more sharpened than in the past
 is chunaav main rahul gandhi apni reliyon main jo kahana chaah rahe hai log use vastav main sun rahe hai
 It sounds strange to hear, but this correspondent himself noticed during the 2014 campaign that people started getting up as soon as Rahul Gandhi started speaking in public meetings
 lekin ab wo sthiti nahin rahi he
 However, if you listen to Modi, Rahul seems pale compared to him
 hamane upi ke hardoi jile main do ghante ke antar par donon ko suna
 Simply put, there is no comparison between the two
 rahul ke pita rajeev gandhi bhi hindi ke ojasvi vaktaa nahin the lekin unke saamne virdohi ke taur par modi jaisi koi chhavi nahin thi
 Despite trying, Rahul Gandhi does not have a cut of Modi's utter eloquence
 8
 Rajnath never denied becoming the CM face of the BJP
 There was a talk that the BJP was going to come out in such a way that Rajnath Singh could be asked to become the face of the party for the CM in UP, but the Home Minister said that Delhi Refuses to leave
 lekin ye mahaj atkal hi sabit hui
 This reporter has reasons to believe that neither Modi nor Shah asked Rajnath Singh to become the face of the party in UP
 grih mantri ke kareebi sutron ke mutabik agar unhen aupchaarik taur par aisa prastaav kiya jaataa to ve sakaaratmak taur par ise sweekaar karte
 The bjp's argument seems to be that upper castes like Thakur, the community from which Rajnath comes, will support the party in any case

 7south delhishri Ramesh bidhurimla Delhi Police Special Cell has arrested Ansar ul Haq, a terrorist of Hizbul Mujahideen, from Delhi Airport for the murder of Police Sub Inspector Imtiaz Ali Mir in Pulwama, Jammu and Kashmir
 ansaarul bangaluru se dilli aayaa tha or apane ghar kashmir ja rahaa tha
 The special cell had been following ansar-ul-haq for several days and was monitoring his movement
 kashmir main SI kii hatyagauratlab he ki 28 oktober ko siaidi ke sab inspector imtiyaaj ahamed mir lambey samay baad mata-pita se milane apane ghar ja rahe the tab raste main vahibag main aatankiyon ne un par firing kar di
 The police had found the body shattered by Imtiaz's bullets
 darasal jammu kashmir main sena aaparishan ol out ke tahat aatankiyon ko chun chun kar thikaane laga rahi he
 Angry terrorists have started targeting the security forces, in this episode, a few days ago, the terrorists made a threat that the police personnel and SPO of the valley should leave their jobs and Imtiaz was killed under the conspiracy after the threat 
 aatanki ne girl friend kaa kiya istemalpulice jaanch main pataa laga ki imtiyaaj kii hatya karne ke liye ansaar ul haq ne apni girl friend kaa istemaal kiya tha

 sadiya sab inspector imtiyaaj ko bhi jaanati thi

 wats ap group se radiclise hokar hi ansaar ne sab inspector kii hatya kii thi
